focus_tree = {
	id = german_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = GER
		}
		modifier = {
			add = -20
			has_global_flag = ger_vanilla_focus_tree
		}
	}

	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = {
		x = 50 y = 1500
	}
	#####DEMO
	focus = {
		id = GER_the_great_red_menace_r56
		icon = GFX_focus_ger_great_red_menace
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_restore_weimar }
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
			any_other_country = {
				original_tag = SOV
				has_government = communism
			}
			has_added_tension_amount < 15
		}
		x = 3
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = GER_restore_weimar
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 8
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_named_threat = { threat = 10 name = GER_the_great_red_menace }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_government = communism
				}
				country_event = { id = wtt_germany.19 days = 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = wtt_news.21 hours = 6 } }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = { is_on_continent = europe }
					NOT = {
						tag = ENG
						tag = FRA
						tag = SWI
						tag = ITA
						tag = IRE
						tag = TUR
						tag = ALB
						original_tag = SPR
						tag = POR
						tag = GRE
						has_government = communism
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = wtt_germany.24 }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = GER_the_great_red_menace days = 1095 }
				add_ai_strategy = {	#A bit too high, don't you think?
					type = befriend
					id = "GER"			
					value = 100
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "ENG"			
					value = -100
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SOV
					has_government = communism
				}
				send_embargo = ROOT
				custom_effect_tooltip = embargo_relation_tt
			}
		}
	}
	focus = {
		id = GER_dem_anschluss_prep 
		icon = GFX_goal_GER_boost_germanism_in_austria
		cost = 5
		prerequisite = {
			focus = GER_the_great_red_menace_r56
		}
		relative_position_id = GER_the_great_red_menace_r56
		x = 2
		y = 1
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			AUS = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_war = no
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism

						is_core_of = HUN
						is_core_of = CZE #despite Germans, wouldnt exclude Sudeten, unlikely scenario
					}
				}
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			AUS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Kurt Schuschnigg"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					retire_country_leader = yes
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.3
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = {
			#
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = GER_central_european_alliance_r56
		icon = GFX_goal_GER_flag_germany_democratic
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_the_great_red_menace_r56 }
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
		}
		
		x = 0
		y = 2
		relative_position_id = GER_the_great_red_menace_r56
		cost = 5
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_central_european_alliance_tt
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_faction = GER_central_european_alliance
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					create_faction = GER_central_european_alliance
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_the_great_red_menace
					has_idea = neutrality_idea
				}
				remove_ideas = neutrality_idea
			}
			else = {
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = wtt_germany.20 days = 1 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = wtt_news.22 hours = 6 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						FRA = { has_government = communism }
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = SPR
							has_government = communism
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "FRA"			
							value = 200
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "FRA"			
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_other_country = {
							original_tag = SOV
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = SOV_getitng_allies_target
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = SPR
							has_government = communism
							NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_hinder_nkvd_interference }
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = event_target:SOV_getitng_allies_target		
							value = 200
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = event_target:SOV_getitng_allies_target				
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FRA = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = SPR
							has_government = fascism
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "FRA"			
							value = 200
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "FRA"			
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SOV = { has_government = fascism } #futureproofing
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = SPR
							has_government = fascism
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "SOV"			
							value = 200
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "SOV"			
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
				# Making England less likely to guarantee European nations.
				ENG = {
					GER_democratic_nations_ai_strategies = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
